# CSES Complete Map

This workbook maps every current CSES Problem Set task to a technique family, prerequisite runway, beginner/intermediate/pro solidifiers, and mutation drills. It is meant to help you solve the whole CSES set without treating it as 400 unrelated puzzles.

Source catalog: [CSES Problem Set](https://cses.fi/problemset/). The catalog was scraped during this session from the live task list.

Total CSES tasks mapped: 400.

## How To Use This

For each target problem:

1. Solve the prerequisite runway first if any item feels shaky.
2. Attempt the target cold.
3. If you fail, read only enough theory to repair the missing concept.
4. Solve the beginner and intermediate solidifiers.
5. Return to the target after 24 hours.
6. Solve the pro solidifier or mutation drills after 7-14 days.

## Repetition Schedule

Use this for every hard or failed CSES problem:

1. Day 0: attempt target after prerequisites.
2. Day 1: redo target from blank editor.
3. Day 3: solve one beginner and one intermediate solidifier.
4. Day 7: solve the target again plus one mutation.
5. Day 14: solve a pro solidifier from the same technique.
6. Day 30: mixed review with five random tasks from different categories.
7. Day 60: teach the pattern out loud and solve a sibling task.

A problem is mastered only when a small mutation does not make you forget the idea.

## Section Counts

- Introductory Problems: 24 tasks
- Sorting and Searching: 35 tasks
- Dynamic Programming: 23 tasks
- Graph Algorithms: 36 tasks
- Range Queries: 25 tasks
- Tree Algorithms: 16 tasks
- Mathematics: 37 tasks
- String Algorithms: 21 tasks
- Geometry: 16 tasks
- Advanced Techniques: 25 tasks
- Sliding Window Problems: 11 tasks
- Interactive Problems: 6 tasks
- Bitwise Operations: 11 tasks
- Construction Problems: 8 tasks
- Advanced Graph Problems: 28 tasks
- Counting Problems: 18 tasks
- Additional Problems I: 30 tasks
- Additional Problems II: 30 tasks

## All-Problem Map

## Introductory Problems

### 1. [Weird Algorithm](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1068)

- Technique family: implementation intro
- Why this matters: This builds the careful implementation base CSES assumes everywhere else.
- Baseline concepts: loops, conditionals, integer bounds, basic arrays/strings
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Length of Last Word](https://leetcode.com/problems/length-of-last-word/), [Plus One](https://leetcode.com/problems/plus-one/), [Valid Parentheses](https://leetcode.com/problems/valid-parentheses/), [Roman to Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/roman-to-integer/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Missing Number](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1083), [Repetitions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1069)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Missing Number](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1083), [Repetitions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1069)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Increasing Array](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1094), [Number Spiral](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1071), [Palindrome Reorder](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1755)
- Pro solidifiers: [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [String Reorder](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1743), [Grid Path Description](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1625)
- Mutation drills:
  - State the invariant before coding.
  - Rewrite with 0-indexed and 1-indexed formulas.
  - Find the largest input that could overflow 32-bit integers.
  - Create three adversarial tests, including minimum and maximum size.

### 5. [Permutations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1070)

- Technique family: constructive intro
- Why this matters: Constructive problems teach you to design an object, not just optimize over one.
- Baseline concepts: constructive reasoning, parity, case splitting, proof by construction
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Valid Parentheses](https://leetcode.com/problems/valid-parentheses/), [Roman to Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/roman-to-integer/), [Palindrome Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/palindrome-number/), [DI String Match](https://leetcode.com/problems/di-string-match/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Two Sets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1092), [Gray Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2205)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Two Sets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1092), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Gray Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2205), [Tower of Hanoi](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2165), [Creating Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1622)
- Pro solidifiers: [Chessboard and Queens](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1624), [Grid Path Description](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1625), [Grid Path Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2418)
- Mutation drills:
  - Prove when construction is impossible.
  - Output lexicographically smallest valid construction.
  - Turn a recursive construction into iterative output.
  - Add a parity or modulo constraint and re-derive the cases.

### 7. [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072)

- Technique family: math formula intro
- Why this matters: Many CSES tasks are short only if you can derive the math instead of simulating.
- Baseline concepts: closed-form formulas, modular arithmetic, counting, parity
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Pow(x, n)](https://leetcode.com/problems/powx-n/), [Sqrt(x)](https://leetcode.com/problems/sqrtx/), [Reverse Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-integer/), [Plus One](https://leetcode.com/problems/plus-one/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Piles](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1754), [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Josephus Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2164)
- Pro solidifiers: [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [Permutation Order](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3397), [Counting Necklaces](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2209)
- Mutation drills:
  - Derive the formula from first principles.
  - Check n=1, n=2, and boundary cases manually.
  - Move from O(n) simulation to O(1) formula.
  - Explain which terms need modulo and which do not.

### 16. [Apple Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1623)

- Technique family: implementation intro
- Why this matters: This builds the careful implementation base CSES assumes everywhere else.
- Baseline concepts: loops, conditionals, integer bounds, basic arrays/strings
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Length of Last Word](https://leetcode.com/problems/length-of-last-word/), [Plus One](https://leetcode.com/problems/plus-one/), [Valid Parentheses](https://leetcode.com/problems/valid-parentheses/), [Roman to Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/roman-to-integer/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Weird Algorithm](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1068), [Missing Number](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1083), [Repetitions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1069)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Weird Algorithm](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1068), [Missing Number](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1083), [Repetitions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1069)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Increasing Array](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1094), [Number Spiral](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1071), [Palindrome Reorder](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1755)
- Pro solidifiers: [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [String Reorder](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1743), [Grid Path Description](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1625)
- Mutation drills:
  - State the invariant before coding.
  - Rewrite with 0-indexed and 1-indexed formulas.
  - Find the largest input that could overflow 32-bit integers.
  - Create three adversarial tests, including minimum and maximum size.

### 17. [Chessboard and Queens](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1624)

- Technique family: constructive intro
- Why this matters: Constructive problems teach you to design an object, not just optimize over one.
- Baseline concepts: constructive reasoning, parity, case splitting, proof by construction
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Valid Parentheses](https://leetcode.com/problems/valid-parentheses/), [Roman to Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/roman-to-integer/), [Palindrome Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/palindrome-number/), [DI String Match](https://leetcode.com/problems/di-string-match/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Permutations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1070), [Two Sets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1092), [Gray Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2205)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Permutations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1070), [Two Sets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1092), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Gray Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2205), [Tower of Hanoi](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2165), [Creating Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1622)
- Pro solidifiers: [Grid Path Description](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1625), [Grid Path Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2418)
- Mutation drills:
  - Prove when construction is impossible.
  - Output lexicographically smallest valid construction.
  - Turn a recursive construction into iterative output.
  - Add a parity or modulo constraint and re-derive the cases.

### 18. [Raab Game I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3399)

- Technique family: math formula intro
- Why this matters: Many CSES tasks are short only if you can derive the math instead of simulating.
- Baseline concepts: closed-form formulas, modular arithmetic, counting, parity
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Pow(x, n)](https://leetcode.com/problems/powx-n/), [Sqrt(x)](https://leetcode.com/problems/sqrtx/), [Reverse Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-integer/), [Plus One](https://leetcode.com/problems/plus-one/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Piles](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1754), [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Josephus Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2164)
- Pro solidifiers: [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [Permutation Order](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3397), [Counting Necklaces](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2209)
- Mutation drills:
  - Derive the formula from first principles.
  - Check n=1, n=2, and boundary cases manually.
  - Move from O(n) simulation to O(1) formula.
  - Explain which terms need modulo and which do not.

## Sorting and Searching

### 25. [Distinct Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1621)

- Technique family: sorting two pointers
- Why this matters: This is the gateway from implementation into efficient O(n log n) reasoning.
- Baseline concepts: sorting, two pointers, frequency/counting, deduplication
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Two Sum II - Input Array Is Sorted](https://leetcode.com/problems/two-sum-ii-input-array-is-sorted/), [3Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/3sum/), [Container With Most Water](https://leetcode.com/problems/container-with-most-water/), [Sort Colors](https://leetcode.com/problems/sort-colors/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Apartments](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1084), [Ferris Wheel](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1090)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Apartments](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1084), [Ferris Wheel](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1090)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Sum of Two Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1640), [Sum of Three Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1641), [Towers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1073)
- Pro solidifiers: [Sum of Four Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1642), [Nested Ranges Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2169), [Movie Festival II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1632)
- Mutation drills:
  - Return indices instead of values.
  - Handle duplicate values without duplicate answers.
  - Change exact sum to closest sum.
  - Generalize 2-sum to 3-sum and 4-sum.

### 28. [Concert Tickets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1091)

- Technique family: ordered sets
- Why this matters: Ordered dynamic state appears across range, sliding-window, geometry, and string-editor tasks.
- Baseline concepts: ordered set, multiset, predecessor/successor, balanced BST
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Contains Duplicate III](https://leetcode.com/problems/contains-duplicate-iii/), [Count of Smaller Numbers After Self](https://leetcode.com/problems/count-of-smaller-numbers-after-self/), [Kth Largest Element in a Stream](https://leetcode.com/problems/kth-largest-element-in-a-stream/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Traffic Lights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1163), [Towers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1073)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Towers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1073), [Josephus Problem I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2162)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Traffic Lights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1163), [Josephus Problem II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2163), [Sliding Window Median](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1076)
- Pro solidifiers: [Sliding Window Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1077), [Salary Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1144), [Cut and Paste](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2072)
- Mutation drills:
  - Replace set with multiset and handle duplicates.
  - Find predecessor and successor after each update.
  - Support deletion as well as insertion.
  - Switch to Fenwick/order-statistics if coordinates are compressible.

### 29. [Restaurant Customers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1619)

- Technique family: greedy intervals
- Why this matters: Greedy CSES problems reward proof discipline more than code volume.
- Baseline concepts: greedy choice, exchange argument, interval sorting, scheduling
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Merge Intervals](https://leetcode.com/problems/merge-intervals/), [Non-overlapping Intervals](https://leetcode.com/problems/non-overlapping-intervals/), [Minimum Number of Arrows to Burst Balloons](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-number-of-arrows-to-burst-balloons/), [Activity Selection](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/activity-selection-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Movie Festival](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1629), [Tasks and Deadlines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1630), [Reading Books](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1631)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Movie Festival](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1629), [Tasks and Deadlines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1630)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Room Allocation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1164), [Movie Festival II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1632), [Nested Ranges Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2168)
- Pro solidifiers: [Movie Festival Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1664), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425), [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402)
- Mutation drills:
  - Write the exchange argument.
  - Sort by end time, start time, and duration; explain which works.
  - Return the selected intervals, not just the count.
  - Add a second resource such as rooms, workers, or machines.

  - Change exact sum to closest sum.
  - Generalize 2-sum to 3-sum and 4-sum.

### 32. [Maximum Subarray Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1643)

- Technique family: subarray prefix
- Why this matters: Prefix-sum thinking is one of the highest-return bridges from easy arrays to hard counting.
- Baseline concepts: prefix sums, subarray counting, hash maps, modulo classes
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Subarray Sum Equals K](https://leetcode.com/problems/subarray-sum-equals-k/), [Range Sum Query - Immutable](https://leetcode.com/problems/range-sum-query-immutable/), [Contiguous Array](https://leetcode.com/problems/contiguous-array/), [Product of Array Except Self](https://leetcode.com/problems/product-of-array-except-self/)

- Mutation drills:
  - Allow negative values and explain why two pointers may fail.
  - Count subarrays instead of finding one.
  - Change exact target to modulo target.
  - Add length bounds and use an ordered structure/deque.

### 35. [Collecting Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2216)

- Technique family: ordered sets
- Why this matters: Ordered dynamic state appears across range, sliding-window, geometry, and string-editor tasks.
- Baseline concepts: ordered set, multiset, predecessor/successor, balanced BST
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Contains Duplicate III](https://leetcode.com/problems/contains-duplicate-iii/), [Count of Smaller Numbers After Self](https://leetcode.com/problems/count-of-smaller-numbers-after-self/), [Kth Largest Element in a Stream](https://leetcode.com/problems/kth-largest-element-in-a-stream/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Concert Tickets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1091), [Traffic Lights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1163), [Towers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1073)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Concert Tickets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1091), [Towers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1073), [Josephus Problem I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2162)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Traffic Lights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1163), [Josephus Problem II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2163), [Sliding Window Median](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1076)
- Pro solidifiers: [Sliding Window Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1077), [Salary Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1144), [Cut and Paste](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2072)
- Mutation drills:
  - Replace set with multiset and handle duplicates.
  - Find predecessor and successor after each update.
  - Support deletion as well as insertion.
  - Switch to Fenwick/order-statistics if coordinates are compressible.

### 44. [Nested Ranges Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2168)

- Technique family: greedy intervals
- Why this matters: Greedy CSES problems reward proof discipline more than code volume.
- Baseline concepts: greedy choice, exchange argument, interval sorting, scheduling
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Merge Intervals](https://leetcode.com/problems/merge-intervals/), [Non-overlapping Intervals](https://leetcode.com/problems/non-overlapping-intervals/), [Minimum Number of Arrows to Burst Balloons](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-number-of-arrows-to-burst-balloons/), [Activity Selection](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/activity-selection-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Movie Festival](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1629), [Tasks and Deadlines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1630), [Reading Books](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1631)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Movie Festival](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1629), [Restaurant Customers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1619), [Tasks and Deadlines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1630)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Room Allocation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1164), [Movie Festival II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1632)
- Pro solidifiers: [Movie Festival Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1664), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425), [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402)
- Mutation drills:
  - Write the exchange argument.
  - Sort by end time, start time, and duration; explain which works.
  - Return the selected intervals, not just the count.
  - Add a second resource such as rooms, workers, or machines.

### 47. [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620)

- Technique family: binary search answer
- Why this matters: Parametric search turns many impossible-looking optimization tasks into clean decision problems.
- Baseline concepts: binary search on answer, monotonic feasibility, count <= x
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Binary Search](https://leetcode.com/problems/binary-search/), [Koko Eating Bananas](https://leetcode.com/problems/koko-eating-bananas/), [Capacity To Ship Packages Within D Days](https://leetcode.com/problems/capacity-to-ship-packages-within-d-days/), [Split Array Largest Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/split-array-largest-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301), [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [K-th Highest Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3305)
- Pro solidifiers: [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088), [Lines and Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3430)
- Mutation drills:
  - Minimize maximum vs maximize minimum.
  - Prove the feasibility predicate is monotonic.
  - Use counting <= mid instead of direct index search.
  - Binary search real values and control precision.

### 48. [Tasks and Deadlines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1630)

- Technique family: greedy intervals
- Why this matters: Greedy CSES problems reward proof discipline more than code volume.
- Baseline concepts: greedy choice, exchange argument, interval sorting, scheduling
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Merge Intervals](https://leetcode.com/problems/merge-intervals/), [Non-overlapping Intervals](https://leetcode.com/problems/non-overlapping-intervals/), [Minimum Number of Arrows to Burst Balloons](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-number-of-arrows-to-burst-balloons/), [Activity Selection](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/activity-selection-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Movie Festival](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1629), [Reading Books](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1631)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Movie Festival](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1629), [Restaurant Customers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1619)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Room Allocation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1164), [Movie Festival II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1632), [Nested Ranges Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2168)
- Pro solidifiers: [Movie Festival Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1664), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425), [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402)
- Mutation drills:
  - Write the exchange argument.
  - Sort by end time, start time, and duration; explain which works.
  - Return the selected intervals, not just the count.
  - Add a second resource such as rooms, workers, or machines.

### 50. [Sum of Three Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1641)

- Technique family: sorting two pointers
- Why this matters: This is the gateway from implementation into efficient O(n log n) reasoning.
- Baseline concepts: sorting, two pointers, frequency/counting, deduplication
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Two Sum II - Input Array Is Sorted](https://leetcode.com/problems/two-sum-ii-input-array-is-sorted/), [3Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/3sum/), [Container With Most Water](https://leetcode.com/problems/container-with-most-water/), [Sort Colors](https://leetcode.com/problems/sort-colors/)

- Mutation drills:
  - Return indices instead of values.
  - Handle duplicate values without duplicate answers.
  - Change exact sum to closest sum.
  - Generalize 2-sum to 3-sum and 4-sum.

### 52. [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645)

- Technique family: monotonic stack
- Why this matters: Monotonic structures are the hidden engine behind many hard linear-time solutions.
- Baseline concepts: monotonic stack, nearest smaller/greater, histogram rectangles, contribution counting
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Next Greater Element I](https://leetcode.com/problems/next-greater-element-i/), [Daily Temperatures](https://leetcode.com/problems/daily-temperatures/), [Largest Rectangle in Histogram](https://leetcode.com/problems/largest-rectangle-in-histogram/), [Trapping Rain Water](https://leetcode.com/problems/trapping-rain-water/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Sliding Window Minimum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3221)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147), [Maximum Building II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1148), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425)
- Pro solidifiers: [Subarray Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1190), [Visible Buildings Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3304), [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch nearest smaller to nearest greater.
  - Handle equal values with strict vs non-strict comparisons.
  - Return boundaries for each index.
  - Convert a grid/sequence into repeated histogram states.

### 53. [Subarray Sums I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1660)

- Technique family: subarray prefix
- Why this matters: Prefix-sum thinking is one of the highest-return bridges from easy arrays to hard counting.
- Baseline concepts: prefix sums, subarray counting, hash maps, modulo classes
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Subarray Sum Equals K](https://leetcode.com/problems/subarray-sum-equals-k/), [Range Sum Query - Immutable](https://leetcode.com/problems/range-sum-query-immutable/), [Contiguous Array](https://leetcode.com/problems/contiguous-array/), [Product of Array Except Self](https://leetcode.com/problems/product-of-array-except-self/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Maximum Subarray Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1643), [Subarray Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1661)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Maximum Subarray Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1643), [Subarray Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1661)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Subarray Divisibility](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1662), [Distinct Values Subarrays II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2428), [Maximum Subarray Sum II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1644)
- Pro solidifiers: [Subarray Squares](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2086), [Subarray Sum Constraints](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3294), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233)
- Mutation drills:
  - Allow negative values and explain why two pointers may fail.
  - Count subarrays instead of finding one.
  - Change exact target to modulo target.
  - Add length bounds and use an ordered structure/deque.

## Dynamic Programming

### 60. [Dice Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1633)

- Technique family: dp coin knapsack
- Why this matters: Knapsack variants are one of the most repeated DP families across CSES and interviews.
- Baseline concepts: 1D DP, knapsack, counting ways, minimization, loop direction
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Coin Change](https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change/), [Coin Change II](https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change-ii/), [Partition Equal Subset Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-equal-subset-sum/), [Target Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/target-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634), [Coin Combinations I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1635)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634), [Coin Combinations I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1635)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Combinations II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1636), [Book Shop](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1158), [Money Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1745)
- Pro solidifiers: [Book Shop II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1159), [Coding Company](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1665), [Same Sum Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3425)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch from min coins to count ways.
  - Switch order-sensitive to order-insensitive counting.
  - Compress a 2D DP to 1D safely.
  - Add a second resource dimension.

### 61. [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634)

- Technique family: dp coin knapsack

### 62. [Coin Combinations I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1635)

- Technique family: dp coin knapsack
- Why this matters: Knapsack variants are one of the most repeated DP families across CSES and interviews.
- Baseline concepts: 1D DP, knapsack, counting ways, minimization, loop direction
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Coin Change](https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change/), [Coin Change II](https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change-ii/), [Partition Equal Subset Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-equal-subset-sum/), [Target Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/target-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Dice Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1633), [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Dice Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1633), [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Combinations II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1636), [Book Shop](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1158), [Money Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1745)
- Pro solidifiers: [Book Shop II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1159), [Coding Company](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1665), [Same Sum Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3425)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch from min coins to count ways.
  - Switch order-sensitive to order-insensitive counting.
  - Compress a 2D DP to 1D safely.
  - Add a second resource dimension.

### 63. [Coin Combinations II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1636)

- Why this matters: Knapsack variants are one of the most repeated DP families across CSES and interviews.

### 64. [Removing Digits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1637)

- Technique family: digit dp
- Why this matters: Digit DP teaches precise state flags and range-count transformations.
- Baseline concepts: digit DP, tight flag, leading zero, position state
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Number of Digit One](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-digit-one/), [Numbers At Most N Given Digit Set](https://leetcode.com/problems/numbers-at-most-n-given-digit-set/), [Count Numbers Less Than N Containing Digits From The Given Set](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/count-numbers-less-than-n-containing-digits-from-the-given-set-digit-dp/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Counting Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2220), [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Counting Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2220), [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [Removing Digits II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2174)
- Pro solidifiers: [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Counting Sequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2228), [Functional Graph Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2415)
- Mutation drills:
  - Answer range [L, R] as f(R)-f(L-1).
  - Add previous digit to the state.
  - Handle leading zeros explicitly.
  - Combine digit DP with automaton state.

### 65. [Grid Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1638)

- Technique family: dp grid
- Why this matters: Grid DP starts simple but leads directly into profile DP and combinatorial counting.
- Baseline concepts: grid DP, path counting, obstacles, state compression
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Unique Paths](https://leetcode.com/problems/unique-paths/), [Minimum Path Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-path-sum/), [Triangle](https://leetcode.com/problems/triangle/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Minimal Grid Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3359), [Grid Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1078)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Minimal Grid Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3359), [Grid Coloring I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3311)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Grid Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1078), [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [Grid Coloring II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3312)
- Pro solidifiers: [Grid Completion](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2429), [Grid Puzzle I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2432), [Grid Puzzle II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2131)
- Mutation drills:
  - Count paths vs minimize path cost.
  - Add obstacles or forbidden cells.
  - Swap dimensions to reduce memory.
  - Encode a row/column frontier as a bitmask.

### 68. [Counting Towers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2413)

- Technique family: dp interval game
- Why this matters: Interval DP is where many solvers first learn that the obvious recursion order is wrong.
- Baseline concepts: interval DP, game DP, choose first/last, optimal substructure over ranges
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Burst Balloons](https://leetcode.com/problems/burst-balloons/), [Minimum Score Triangulation of Polygon](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-score-triangulation-of-polygon/), [Matrix Chain Multiplication](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-chain-multiplication0303/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Rectangle Cutting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1744), [Removal Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1097), [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Rectangle Cutting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1744), [Removal Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1097)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080), [Permutation Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2229), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088)
- Pro solidifiers: [Stick Difference](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3401), [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402), [Reversal Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2075)
- Mutation drills:
  - Choose the last action instead of the first.
  - Represent score difference instead of both scores.
  - Add a third state if outside context matters.
  - Test all intervals by increasing length.

### 69. [Edit Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1639)

- Technique family: dp string
- Why this matters: String DP teaches state design under two dimensions and pattern constraints.
- Baseline concepts: string DP, edit distance, LCS, automata-assisted DP
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Edit Distance](https://leetcode.com/problems/edit-distance/), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-common-subsequence/), [Longest Palindromic Subsequence](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-palindromic-subsequence/), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/longest-common-subsequence-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Longest Common Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3403), [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Longest Common Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3403), [Word Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1731)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Distinct Subsequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1149), [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080)
- Pro solidifiers: [String Transform](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1113), [Substring Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2110), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103)
- Mutation drills:
  - Define dp[i][j] precisely before coding.
  - Return reconstruction, not just length/count.
  - Move from substring DP to automaton state DP.
  - Space-compress when only previous row is needed.

### 78. [Projects](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1140)

- Technique family: dp coin knapsack
- Why this matters: Knapsack variants are one of the most repeated DP families across CSES and interviews.
- Baseline concepts: 1D DP, knapsack, counting ways, minimization, loop direction
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Coin Change](https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change/), [Coin Change II](https://leetcode.com/problems/coin-change-ii/), [Partition Equal Subset Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-equal-subset-sum/), [Target Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/target-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Dice Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1633), [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634), [Coin Combinations I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1635)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Dice Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1633), [Minimizing Coins](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1634), [Coin Combinations I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1635)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Combinations II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1636), [Book Shop](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1158), [Money Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1745)
- Pro solidifiers: [Book Shop II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1159), [Coding Company](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1665), [Same Sum Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3425)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch from min coins to count ways.
  - Switch order-sensitive to order-insensitive counting.
  - Compress a 2D DP to 1D safely.
  - Add a second resource dimension.

### 79. [Elevator Rides](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1653)

- Technique family: dp bitmask profile
- Why this matters: Bitmask and profile DP are the bridge into serious competitive-programming DP.
- Baseline concepts: bitmask DP, subset DP, profile DP, state compression
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Beautiful Arrangement](https://leetcode.com/problems/beautiful-arrangement/), [Partition to K Equal Sum Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-to-k-equal-sum-subsets/), [Parallel Courses II](https://leetcode.com/problems/parallel-courses-ii/), [Travelling Salesman Problem](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/travelling-salesman-problem2732/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [Hamiltonian Flights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1690)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [School Excursion](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1706)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Hamiltonian Flights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1690), [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [K Subset Sums I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3108)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3109), [Grid Puzzle II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2131), [Same Sum Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3425)
- Mutation drills:
  - Mask represents used items, skills, or frontier cells.
  - Iterate submasks efficiently.
  - Precompute transitions or subset scores.
  - Reconstruct the chosen subset/path.

### 80. [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181)

- Technique family: dp grid
- Why this matters: Grid DP starts simple but leads directly into profile DP and combinatorial counting.
- Baseline concepts: grid DP, path counting, obstacles, state compression
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Unique Paths](https://leetcode.com/problems/unique-paths/), [Minimum Path Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-path-sum/), [Triangle](https://leetcode.com/problems/triangle/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Grid Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1638), [Minimal Grid Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3359), [Grid Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1078)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Grid Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1638), [Minimal Grid Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3359), [Grid Coloring I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3311)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Grid Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1078), [Grid Coloring II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3312)
- Pro solidifiers: [Grid Completion](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2429), [Grid Puzzle I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2432), [Grid Puzzle II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2131)
- Mutation drills:
  - Count paths vs minimize path cost.
  - Add obstacles or forbidden cells.
  - Swap dimensions to reduce memory.
  - Encode a row/column frontier as a bitmask.

### 81. [Counting Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2220)

- Technique family: digit dp
- Why this matters: Digit DP teaches precise state flags and range-count transformations.
- Baseline concepts: digit DP, tight flag, leading zero, position state
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Number of Digit One](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-digit-one/), [Numbers At Most N Given Digit Set](https://leetcode.com/problems/numbers-at-most-n-given-digit-set/), [Count Numbers Less Than N Containing Digits From The Given Set](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/count-numbers-less-than-n-containing-digits-from-the-given-set-digit-dp/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [Removing Digits II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2174)
- Pro solidifiers: [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Counting Sequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2228), [Functional Graph Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2415)
- Mutation drills:
  - Answer range [L, R] as f(R)-f(L-1).
  - Add previous digit to the state.
  - Handle leading zeros explicitly.
  - Combine digit DP with automaton state.

### 82. [Increasing Subsequence II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1748)

- Technique family: dp string
- Why this matters: String DP teaches state design under two dimensions and pattern constraints.
- Baseline concepts: string DP, edit distance, LCS, automata-assisted DP
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Edit Distance](https://leetcode.com/problems/edit-distance/), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-common-subsequence/), [Longest Palindromic Subsequence](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-palindromic-subsequence/), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/longest-common-subsequence-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Edit Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1639), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3403), [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Edit Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1639), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3403), [Word Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1731)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Distinct Subsequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1149), [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080)
- Pro solidifiers: [String Transform](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1113), [Substring Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2110), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103)
- Mutation drills:
  - Define dp[i][j] precisely before coding.
  - Return reconstruction, not just length/count.
  - Move from substring DP to automaton state DP.
  - Space-compress when only previous row is needed.

## Graph Algorithms

### 83. [Counting Rooms](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1192)

- Technique family: graph bfs dfs
- Why this matters: Graph basics are the language for nearly every advanced CSES graph task.
- Baseline concepts: DFS, BFS, components, parent reconstruction, grid graph
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Number of Islands](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-islands/), [Clone Graph](https://leetcode.com/problems/clone-graph/), [Rotting Oranges](https://leetcode.com/problems/rotting-oranges/), [Number of Provinces](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-provinces/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Labyrinth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1193), [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Labyrinth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1193), [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Message Route](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1667), [Building Teams](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1668), [Round Trip](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1669)
- Pro solidifiers: [Monsters](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1194), [Swap Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1670), [Graph Girth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1707)
- Mutation drills:
  - Reconstruct a shortest path.
  - Run multi-source BFS.
  - Detect an undirected cycle.
  - Turn a grid into an implicit graph.

### 85. [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666)

- Technique family: mst dsu
- Why this matters: DSU starts easy and becomes a core technique for offline and graph-optimization tasks.
- Baseline concepts: DSU, Kruskal, component size, MST edge classification
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Min Cost to Connect All Points](https://leetcode.com/problems/min-cost-to-connect-all-points/), [Redundant Connection](https://leetcode.com/problems/redundant-connection/), [Minimum Spanning Tree - Kruskal's Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/minimum-spanning-tree-kruskals-algorithm/1), [Disjoint Set (Union-Find)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/disjoint-set-union-find/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676), [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407), [MST Edge Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3409)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [New Roads Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2101), [Transfer Speeds Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3111)
- Mutation drills:
  - Maintain component count and max component size.
  - Force or ban one edge in MST.
  - Process deletions offline in reverse.
  - Classify critical and optional MST edges.

### 90. [Shortest Routes I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1671)

- Technique family: graph shortest paths
- Why this matters: Shortest path variations teach algorithm selection under edge-weight constraints.
- Baseline concepts: Dijkstra, Bellman-Ford, Floyd-Warshall, k-shortest paths, stateful shortest path
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Network Delay Time](https://leetcode.com/problems/network-delay-time/), [Cheapest Flights Within K Stops](https://leetcode.com/problems/cheapest-flights-within-k-stops/), [Find the City With the Smallest Number of Neighbors at a Threshold Distance](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-city-with-the-smallest-number-of-neighbors-at-a-threshold-distance/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Shortest Routes II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1672), [High Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1673)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Shortest Routes II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1672), [Flight Discount](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1195)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [High Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1673), [Cycle Finding](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1197), [Flight Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1196)
- Pro solidifiers: [Investigation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1202), [Fixed Length Walk Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3357), [Graph Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1724)
- Mutation drills:
  - Negative edges require Bellman-Ford.
  - All-pairs shortest path suggests Floyd-Warshall.
  - Count number of shortest paths.
  - Add one coupon, time budget, or k-route state.

  - Count number of shortest paths.

- Technique family: graph bfs dfs

- Baseline concepts: DFS, BFS, components, parent reconstruction, grid graph

  - Reconstruct a shortest path.
  - Run multi-source BFS.
  - Detect an undirected cycle.
  - Turn a grid into an implicit graph.

### 97. [Course Schedule](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1679)

- Technique family: graph dag toposort
- Why this matters: DAG DP is the bridge between graph traversal and dynamic programming.
- Baseline concepts: topological sort, DAG DP, cycle detection, path counting
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Course Schedule](https://leetcode.com/problems/course-schedule/), [Course Schedule II](https://leetcode.com/problems/course-schedule-ii/), [Find Eventual Safe States](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-eventual-safe-states/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Longest Flight Route](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1680), [Game Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1681)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Round Trip II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1678), [Longest Flight Route](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1680)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Game Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1681), [Course Schedule II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1757), [Acyclic Graph Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1756)
- Pro solidifiers: [Coin Collector](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1686), [Fixed Length Walk Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3357), [Visiting Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1203)
- Mutation drills:
  - Return order, longest path, or path count.
  - Detect cycles before DP.
  - Condense SCCs to create a DAG.
  - Use topo order from indegrees or DFS finish time.

### 101. [Planets Queries I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1750)

- Technique family: functional graph
- Why this matters: Functional graphs show up whenever every node has exactly one outgoing transition.
- Baseline concepts: functional graph, cycle detection, binary lifting, distance to cycle

- Mutation drills:
  - Find kth successor.
  - Find cycle entry and cycle length.
  - Separate tree-in and cycle nodes.
  - Use binary lifting over next pointers.

### 104. [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675)

- Technique family: mst dsu
- Why this matters: DSU starts easy and becomes a core technique for offline and graph-optimization tasks.
- Baseline concepts: DSU, Kruskal, component size, MST edge classification
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Min Cost to Connect All Points](https://leetcode.com/problems/min-cost-to-connect-all-points/), [Redundant Connection](https://leetcode.com/problems/redundant-connection/), [Minimum Spanning Tree - Kruskal's Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/minimum-spanning-tree-kruskals-algorithm/1), [Disjoint Set (Union-Find)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/disjoint-set-union-find/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676), [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407), [MST Edge Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3409)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [New Roads Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2101), [Transfer Speeds Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3111)
- Mutation drills:
  - Maintain component count and max component size.
  - Force or ban one edge in MST.
  - Process deletions offline in reverse.
  - Classify critical and optional MST edges.

### 106. [Flight Routes Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1682)

- Technique family: scc twosat
- Why this matters: SCC is the key that unlocks directed graph structure beyond simple DFS.
- Baseline concepts: SCC, condensation DAG, 2-SAT, reachability
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Strongly Connected Components (Kosaraju's Algo)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/strongly-connected-components-kosarajus-algo/1), [2-Satisfiability (2-SAT) Problem](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/2-satisfiability-2-sat-problem/), [Critical Connections in a Network](https://leetcode.com/problems/critical-connections-in-a-network/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Planets and Kingdoms](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1683), [Giant Pizza](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1684)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Planets and Kingdoms](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1683), [Reachable Nodes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2138)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Giant Pizza](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1684), [Coin Collector](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1686), [Reachability Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2143)
- Pro solidifiers: [New Flight Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1685), [Strongly Connected Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2177), [Critical Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1703)
- Mutation drills:
  - Condense SCCs into a DAG.
  - Solve implications using SCC order.
  - Answer reachability after condensation.
  - Find source/sink SCCs for adding edges.

### 110. [Mail Delivery](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1691)

- Technique family: euler paths
- Why this matters: Euler problems train you to reason about edges, not vertices.
- Baseline concepts: Euler path/circuit, degree conditions, Hierholzer, edge visitation
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Reconstruct Itinerary](https://leetcode.com/problems/reconstruct-itinerary/), [Euler Circuit and Path](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/euler-circuit-and-path/1), [Euler Circuit in a Directed Graph](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/euler-circuit-directed-graph/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Teleporters Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1693), [De Bruijn Sequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1692)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Teleporters Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1693), Reconstruct Itinerary-style path
- Intermediate solidifiers: [De Bruijn Sequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1692), [Split into Two Paths](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3358), [Eulerian Subgraphs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2078)
- Pro solidifiers: [Distinct Routes II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2130), [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428), [Network Renovation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1704)
- Mutation drills:
  - Directed vs undirected Euler condition.
  - Use every edge exactly once.
  - Construct path after dead ends.
  - Prefer lexicographically smallest edge if required.

- Technique family: graph bfs dfs

### 115. [Download Speed](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1694)

- Technique family: flow matching
- Why this matters: Flow is the doorway to matching, cuts, disjoint paths, and assignment-style reductions.
- Baseline concepts: max flow, min cut, bipartite matching, path decomposition
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Is Graph Bipartite?](https://leetcode.com/problems/is-graph-bipartite/), [Find the Maximum Flow](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/find-the-maximum-flow2126/1), [Maximum Bipartite Matching](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/maximum-bipartite-matching--170646/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Police Chase](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1695), [School Dance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1696)
- Beginner solidifiers: [School Dance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1696), [Police Chase](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1695)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Distinct Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1711), [Grid Puzzle I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2432), [Grid Puzzle II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2131)
- Pro solidifiers: [Task Assignment](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2129), [Parcel Delivery](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2121), [Distinct Routes II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2130)
- Mutation drills:
  - Extract min cut after max flow.
  - Reduce matching to flow.
  - Recover actual disjoint paths.
  - Add capacities greater than one.

## Range Queries

### 119. [Static Range Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1646)

- Technique family: range prefix sparse
- Why this matters: Static range query tools are the baseline for faster dynamic structures.
- Baseline concepts: prefix sums, 2D prefix, sparse table, idempotent range queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Sparse Table](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/sparse-table/), [Range Minimum Query (Square Root Decomposition and Sparse Table)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/range-minimum-query-for-static-array/), [Sliding Window Maximum](https://leetcode.com/problems/sliding-window-maximum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Static Range Minimum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1647), [Forest Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1652)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Static Range Minimum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1647), [Range Xor Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1650)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Forest Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1652), [Visible Buildings Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3304), [Range Interval Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3163)
- Pro solidifiers: [Increasing Array Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2416), [Movie Festival Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1664), [Missing Coin Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2184)
- Mutation drills:
  - Static vs dynamic queries.
  - 2D prefix sum for rectangle queries.
  - Idempotent operations allow overlapping sparse blocks.
  - Explain why sum cannot use sparse overlap like min.

### 121. [Dynamic Range Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1648)

- Technique family: segment tree lazy
- Why this matters: Segment trees are CSES's central dynamic range-query workhorse.
- Baseline concepts: segment tree, lazy propagation, range assignment/addition, custom node merge
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Range Sum Query - Mutable](https://leetcode.com/problems/range-sum-query-mutable/), [Handling Sum Queries After Update](https://leetcode.com/problems/handling-sum-queries-after-update/), [My Calendar III](https://leetcode.com/problems/my-calendar-iii/), [Matrix Exponentiation](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-exponentiation2711/1)

- Intermediate solidifiers: [Pizzeria Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2206), [Subarray Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1190), [Forest Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1739)
- Pro solidifiers: [Range Updates and Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1735), [Polynomial Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1736), [Range Queries and Copies](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1737)
- Mutation drills:
  - Range add and range sum.
  - Range assign and range minimum.
  - Maintain max prefix/suffix/best subarray.
  - Path-copy nodes for persistence.

### 124. [Range Update Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1651)

- Technique family: fenwick order
- Why this matters: Fenwick trees make many offline counting and order-statistics tasks practical.
- Baseline concepts: Fenwick tree, coordinate compression, order statistics, offline queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Range Sum Query - Mutable](https://leetcode.com/problems/range-sum-query-mutable/), [Count of Smaller Numbers After Self](https://leetcode.com/problems/count-of-smaller-numbers-after-self/), [Count Inversions](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/inversion-of-array-1587115620/1)

- Pro solidifiers: [Distinct Values Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3356), [Sliding Window Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3223), [K Subset Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3109)
- Mutation drills:
  - Point update plus prefix query.
  - Range update plus point query.
  - Find kth active element.
  - Compress values before Fenwick operations.

### 126. [Hotel Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1143)

- Technique family: segment tree lazy

- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Range Sum Query - Mutable](https://leetcode.com/problems/range-sum-query-mutable/), [Handling Sum Queries After Update](https://leetcode.com/problems/handling-sum-queries-after-update/), [My Calendar III](https://leetcode.com/problems/my-calendar-iii/), [Matrix Exponentiation](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-exponentiation2711/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Dynamic Range Minimum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1649), [Hotel Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1143), [Prefix Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2166)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Dynamic Range Minimum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1649), [Hotel Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1143), [Prefix Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2166)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Pizzeria Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2206), [Subarray Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1190), [Forest Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1739)
- Pro solidifiers: [Range Updates and Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1735), [Range Queries and Copies](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1737)
- Mutation drills:
  - Range add and range sum.
  - Range assign and range minimum.
  - Maintain max prefix/suffix/best subarray.
  - Path-copy nodes for persistence.

## Tree Algorithms

### 144. [Subordinates](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1674)

- Technique family: tree basics
- Why this matters: Tree basics establish the DFS return-value discipline needed for every advanced tree task.
- Baseline concepts: tree DFS, subtree size, diameter, tree DP
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Maximum Depth of Binary Tree](https://leetcode.com/problems/maximum-depth-of-binary-tree/), [Diameter of Binary Tree](https://leetcode.com/problems/diameter-of-binary-tree/), [Binary Tree Level Order Traversal](https://leetcode.com/problems/binary-tree-level-order-traversal/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Tree Diameter](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1131), [Tree Matching](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1130)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Tree Diameter](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1131), [Tree Matching](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1130)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Tree Distances I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1132), [Tree Distances II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1133), [Finding a Centroid](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2079)
- Pro solidifiers: [Tree Coin Collecting I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3114), [Tree Coin Collecting II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3149), [Network Renovation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1704)
- Mutation drills:
  - Root the tree and compute subtree info.
  - Use two DFS passes for diameter.
  - Keep selected/not-selected states.
  - Reroot answer from parent to child.

### 147. [Tree Distances I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1132)

- Technique family: lca binary lifting
- Why this matters: Binary lifting is a reusable precomputation pattern for trees and functional graphs.
- Baseline concepts: binary lifting, LCA, path distance, ancestor jumps
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Lowest Common Ancestor of a Binary Tree](https://leetcode.com/problems/lowest-common-ancestor-of-a-binary-tree/), [LCA in Binary Tree](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/lowest-common-ancestor-in-a-binary-tree/1), [Kth Ancestor of a Tree Node](https://leetcode.com/problems/kth-ancestor-of-a-tree-node/), [Lowest Common Ancestor in a BST](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/lowest-common-ancestor-in-a-bst/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Company Queries I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1687), [Company Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1688), [Distance Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1135)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Company Queries I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1687), [Company Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1688), [Distance Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1135)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Counting Paths](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1136), [Planets Queries I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1750), [Planets Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1160)
- Pro solidifiers: [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705), [Critical Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1703), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702)
- Mutation drills:
  - Lift deeper node first.
  - Jump by powers of two.
  - Compute distance using depths and LCA.
  - Use difference counts on paths.

### 153. [Subtree Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1137)

- Technique family: tree queries hld
- Why this matters: This is the main transition from tree DP to data structures on trees.
- Baseline concepts: Euler tour, subtree flattening, HLD, path queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Kth Ancestor of a Tree Node](https://leetcode.com/problems/kth-ancestor-of-a-tree-node/), [Implementation of Heavy Light Decomposition](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/implementation-of-heavy-light-decomposition/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Path Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1138), [Path Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2134)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Path Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1138), [Distinct Colors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1139)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Path Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2134), [Counting Paths](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1136), [Distinct Colors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1139)
- Pro solidifiers: [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705), [Network Renovation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1704), [Creating Offices](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1752)
- Mutation drills:
  - Subtree queries become one interval.
  - Path queries become O(log n) heavy segments.
  - Handle node values vs edge values.
  - Combine HLD with segment tree.

- Prerequisite runway: [Subtree Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1137), [Path Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1138), [Path Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2134)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Subtree Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1137), [Path Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1138)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Path Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2134), [Counting Paths](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1136)
- Pro solidifiers: [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705), [Network Renovation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1704), [Creating Offices](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1752)
- Mutation drills:
  - Subtree queries become one interval.
  - Path queries become O(log n) heavy segments.
  - Handle node values vs edge values.
  - Combine HLD with segment tree.

### 157. [Finding a Centroid](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2079)

- Technique family: centroid decomposition
- Why this matters: Centroid methods open a new class of tree path-counting problems.
- Baseline concepts: centroid, divide and conquer on tree, path counting, distance frequency
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Centroid Decomposition of Tree](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/centroid-decomposition-of-tree/), [Diameter of Binary Tree](https://leetcode.com/problems/diameter-of-binary-tree/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Fixed-Length Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2080), [Fixed-Length Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2081)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Fixed-Length Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2080), [Tree Distances I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1132)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Fixed-Length Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2081), [Tree Distances II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1133), [Counting Paths](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1136)
- Pro solidifiers: [Creating Offices](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1752), [Tree Coin Collecting II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3149), [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705)
- Mutation drills:
  - Find centroid by subtree sizes.
  - Count paths through current centroid.
  - Avoid double counting within one child subtree.
  - Maintain distance frequencies.

## Mathematics

### 160. [Josephus Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2164)

- Technique family: math formula intro
- Why this matters: Many CSES tasks are short only if you can derive the math instead of simulating.
- Baseline concepts: closed-form formulas, modular arithmetic, counting, parity
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Pow(x, n)](https://leetcode.com/problems/powx-n/), [Sqrt(x)](https://leetcode.com/problems/sqrtx/), [Reverse Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-integer/), [Plus One](https://leetcode.com/problems/plus-one/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Piles](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1754), [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431)
- Pro solidifiers: [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [Permutation Order](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3397), [Counting Necklaces](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2209)
- Mutation drills:
  - Derive the formula from first principles.
  - Check n=1, n=2, and boundary cases manually.
  - Move from O(n) simulation to O(1) formula.
  - Explain which terms need modulo and which do not.

### 161. [Exponentiation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1095)

- Technique family: mod combinatorics
- Why this matters: Combinatorics problems are short only after the counting model is clear.
- Baseline concepts: modular exponentiation, factorials, modular inverse, combinatorics
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [nCr](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/ncr1019/1), [nCr mod M | Part 1](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/ncr-mod-m-part-10038/1), [nCr mod M | Part 2](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/ncr-mod-m-part-20611/1), [Modular Inverse](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/modular-multiplicative-inverse-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Exponentiation II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1712), [Binomial Coefficients](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1079)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Exponentiation II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1712), [Binomial Coefficients](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1079)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Creating Strings II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1715), [Distributing Apples](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1716), [Christmas Party](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1717)
- Pro solidifiers: [Bracket Sequences II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2187), [Counting Necklaces](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2209), [Counting Grids](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2210)
- Mutation drills:
  - Precompute factorial and inverse factorial.
  - Use Fermat inverse under prime modulo.
  - Divide by duplicate factorials.
  - Apply Burnside when rotations/reflections appear.

### 163. [Counting Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1713)

- Technique family: number theory
- Why this matters: Number theory tasks reward changing perspective from numbers to factors/divisors.
- Baseline concepts: sieve, divisors, prime factorization, gcd, inclusion-exclusion
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Count Primes](https://leetcode.com/problems/count-primes/), [Sieve of Eratosthenes](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/sieve-of-eratosthenes5242/1), [Find Greatest Common Divisor of Array](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-greatest-common-divisor-of-array/), [Modular Inverse](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/modular-multiplicative-inverse-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Common Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1081), [Sum of Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1082)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Common Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1081), [Next Prime](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3396)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Sum of Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1082), [Divisor Analysis](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2182), [Prime Multiples](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2185)
- Pro solidifiers: [Counting Coprime Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2417), [Counting LCM Arrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3169), [GCD Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3161)
- Mutation drills:
  - Precompute smallest prime factors.
  - Count by multiples instead of pairs.
  - Use inclusion-exclusion over prime factors.
  - Separate value frequency from divisor frequency.

### 180. [Fibonacci Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1722)

- Technique family: matrix probability games
- Why this matters: This section ties math, DP, and game theory into compact but deep tasks.
- Baseline concepts: matrix exponentiation, linear recurrences, probability DP, Grundy/nim
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Nim Game](https://leetcode.com/problems/nim-game/), [Stone Game](https://leetcode.com/problems/stone-game/), [New 21 Game](https://leetcode.com/problems/new-21-game/), [Matrix Exponentiation](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-exponentiation2711/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Throwing Dice](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1096), [Dice Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1725)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Throwing Dice](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1096), [Dice Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1725)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Graph Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1723), [Graph Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1724), [Moving Robots](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1726)
- Pro solidifiers: [System of Linear Equations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3154), [Inversion Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1728), [Grundy's Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2207)
- Mutation drills:
  - Turn recurrence into matrix transitions.
  - Use min-plus multiplication for shortest path counts/costs.
  - Compute expectation/probability by state DP.
  - Use xor of Grundy numbers for impartial games.

### 185. [Sum of Four Squares](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3355)

- Technique family: number theory
- Why this matters: Number theory tasks reward changing perspective from numbers to factors/divisors.
- Baseline concepts: sieve, divisors, prime factorization, gcd, inclusion-exclusion
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Count Primes](https://leetcode.com/problems/count-primes/), [Sieve of Eratosthenes](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/sieve-of-eratosthenes5242/1), [Find Greatest Common Divisor of Array](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-greatest-common-divisor-of-array/), [Modular Inverse](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/modular-multiplicative-inverse-1587115620/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Counting Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1713), [Common Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1081), [Sum of Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1082)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1713), [Common Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1081), [Next Prime](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3396)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Sum of Divisors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1082), [Divisor Analysis](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2182), [Prime Multiples](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2185)
- Pro solidifiers: [Counting Coprime Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2417), [Counting LCM Arrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3169), [GCD Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3161)
- Mutation drills:
  - Precompute smallest prime factors.
  - Count by multiples instead of pairs.
  - Use inclusion-exclusion over prime factors.
  - Separate value frequency from divisor frequency.

### 186. [Triangle Number Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3406)

- Technique family: math formula intro
- Why this matters: Many CSES tasks are short only if you can derive the math instead of simulating.
- Baseline concepts: closed-form formulas, modular arithmetic, counting, parity
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Pow(x, n)](https://leetcode.com/problems/powx-n/), [Sqrt(x)](https://leetcode.com/problems/sqrtx/), [Reverse Integer](https://leetcode.com/problems/reverse-integer/), [Plus One](https://leetcode.com/problems/plus-one/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Two Knights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1072), [Bit Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1617), [Trailing Zeros](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1618)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Coin Piles](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1754), [Digit Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2431), [Josephus Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2164)
- Pro solidifiers: [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [Permutation Order](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3397), [Counting Necklaces](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2209)
- Mutation drills:
  - Derive the formula from first principles.
  - Check n=1, n=2, and boundary cases manually.
  - Move from O(n) simulation to O(1) formula.
  - Explain which terms need modulo and which do not.

### 187. [Dice Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1725)

- Technique family: matrix probability games
- Why this matters: This section ties math, DP, and game theory into compact but deep tasks.
- Baseline concepts: matrix exponentiation, linear recurrences, probability DP, Grundy/nim

- Mutation drills:
  - Turn recurrence into matrix transitions.
  - Use min-plus multiplication for shortest path counts/costs.
  - Compute expectation/probability by state DP.
  - Use xor of Grundy numbers for impartial games.

## String Algorithms

### 197. [Word Combinations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1731)

- Technique family: strings kmp hash
- Why this matters: String algorithms turn repeated substring comparisons into reusable structure.
- Baseline concepts: KMP, Z-function, rolling hash, borders/periods
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Find the Index of the First Occurrence in a String](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-index-of-the-first-occurrence-in-a-string/), [Repeated Substring Pattern](https://leetcode.com/problems/repeated-substring-pattern/), [Search Pattern (KMP-Algorithm)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/search-pattern0205/1), [Prefix Function and KMP Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/prefix-function-and-kmp-algorithm-for-competitive-programming/)
- Prerequisite runway: [String Matching](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1753), [Finding Borders](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1732), [Finding Periods](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1733)
- Beginner solidifiers: [String Matching](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1753), [Finding Borders](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1732), [Finding Periods](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1733)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [String Functions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2107), [Palindrome Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2420), [Special Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2186)
- Pro solidifiers: [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103), [String Transform](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1113)
- Mutation drills:
  - Compute prefix-function and Z-array.
  - Find all borders and periods.
  - Use double hashing for collision safety.
  - Combine automaton state with DP.
