- Intermediate solidifiers: [String Functions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2107), [Palindrome Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2420), [Special Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2186)
- Pro solidifiers: [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103), [String Transform](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1113)
- Mutation drills:
  - Compute prefix-function and Z-array.
  - Find all borders and periods.
  - Use double hashing for collision safety.
  - Combine automaton state with DP.

### 202. [Longest Palindrome](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1111)

- Technique family: palindromes
- Why this matters: Palindrome tasks teach center expansion, radii, hashing, and interval reasoning.
- Baseline concepts: Manacher, palindrome radii, palindrome DP, hash palindrome queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Longest Palindromic Substring](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-palindromic-substring/), [Palindromic Substrings](https://leetcode.com/problems/palindromic-substrings/), [Longest Palindromic Substring](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/longest-palindromic-substring-in-linear-time/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [All Palindromes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3138), [Palindrome Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2420)
- Beginner solidifiers: [All Palindromes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3138), [Palindrome Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2420)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080), [Required Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1112), [Special Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2186)
- Pro solidifiers: [Distinct Subsequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1149), [String Transform](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1113), [Substring Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2110)
- Mutation drills:
  - Handle odd and even palindromes.
  - Answer palindrome substring queries.
  - Count palindromes instead of finding longest.
  - Use hashing or Manacher depending on update/static needs.

### 212. [String Functions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2107)

- Technique family: strings kmp hash
- Why this matters: String algorithms turn repeated substring comparisons into reusable structure.
- Baseline concepts: KMP, Z-function, rolling hash, borders/periods
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Find the Index of the First Occurrence in a String](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-index-of-the-first-occurrence-in-a-string/), [Repeated Substring Pattern](https://leetcode.com/problems/repeated-substring-pattern/), [Search Pattern (KMP-Algorithm)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/search-pattern0205/1), [Prefix Function and KMP Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/prefix-function-and-kmp-algorithm-for-competitive-programming/)

- Mutation drills:
  - Compute prefix-function and Z-array.
  - Find all borders and periods.
  - Use double hashing for collision safety.
  - Combine automaton state with DP.

- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Longest Duplicate Substring](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-duplicate-substring/), [Suffix Array](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/suffix-array-set-1-introduction/), [Implement strStr()](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-index-of-the-first-occurrence-in-a-string/), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-common-subsequence/)

- Beginner solidifiers: [Finding Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2102), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103), [Pattern Positions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2104)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Distinct Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2105), [Repeating Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2106), [Substring Order I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2108)
- Pro solidifiers: [Inverse Suffix Array](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3225), [Substring Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2110)
- Mutation drills:
  - Count distinct substrings using LCP.
  - Find kth lexicographic substring.
  - Use automaton/failure links for many patterns.
  - Compare suffix array and suffix automaton approaches.

### 217. [Substring Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2110)

- Technique family: strings suffix automata
- Why this matters: This is where CSES strings become competitive-programming strings.
- Baseline concepts: suffix array, LCP, Aho-Corasick, substring counting/order
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Longest Duplicate Substring](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-duplicate-substring/), [Suffix Array](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/suffix-array-set-1-introduction/), [Implement strStr()](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-index-of-the-first-occurrence-in-a-string/), [Longest Common Subsequence](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-common-subsequence/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Finding Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2102), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103), [Distinct Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2105)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Finding Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2102), [Counting Patterns](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2103), [Pattern Positions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2104)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Distinct Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2105), [Repeating Substring](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2106), [Substring Order I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2108)
- Pro solidifiers: [Inverse Suffix Array](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3225), [Substring Order II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2109)
- Mutation drills:
  - Count distinct substrings using LCP.
  - Find kth lexicographic substring.
  - Use automaton/failure links for many patterns.
  - Compare suffix array and suffix automaton approaches.

## Geometry

### 218. [Point Location Test](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2189)

- Technique family: geometry basic
- Why this matters: Geometry becomes manageable when every decision is an orientation test.
- Baseline concepts: orientation, cross product, line intersection, polygon area
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Check If It Is a Straight Line](https://leetcode.com/problems/check-if-it-is-a-straight-line/), [Largest Triangle Area](https://leetcode.com/problems/largest-triangle-area/), [Max Points on a Line](https://leetcode.com/problems/max-points-on-a-line/)

- Mutation drills:
  - Avoid floating-point slopes.
  - Handle collinear points.
  - Use signed area.
  - Check boundary cases separately.

### 225. [Maximum Manhattan Distances](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3410)

- Technique family: geometry advanced
- Why this matters: Advanced geometry combines coordinate transforms with data structures.
- Baseline concepts: sweep line, Manhattan transform, convex hull, rectangle union
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Convex Hull](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/convex-hull2138/1), [Erect the Fence](https://leetcode.com/problems/erect-the-fence/), [Max Points on a Line](https://leetcode.com/problems/max-points-on-a-line/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Convex Hull](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2195), [Intersection Points](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1740)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Convex Hull](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2195), [All Manhattan Distances](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3411)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Intersection Points](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1740), [Area of Rectangles](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1741), [Robot Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1742)
- Pro solidifiers: [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428), [Lines and Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3430), [Nearest Campsites II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3307)
- Mutation drills:
  - Transform Manhattan distance by x+y and x-y.
  - Sweep one axis and maintain active intervals.
  - Coordinate compress rectangle edges.
  - Use hull/order structure for line queries.

- Pro solidifiers: [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428), [Lines and Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3430), [Nearest Campsites II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3307)
- Mutation drills:
  - Transform Manhattan distance by x+y and x-y.
  - Sweep one axis and maintain active intervals.
  - Coordinate compress rectangle edges.
  - Use hull/order structure for line queries.

### 233. [Robot Path](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1742)

- Technique family: geometry advanced
- Why this matters: Advanced geometry combines coordinate transforms with data structures.
- Baseline concepts: sweep line, Manhattan transform, convex hull, rectangle union
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Convex Hull](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/convex-hull2138/1), [Erect the Fence](https://leetcode.com/problems/erect-the-fence/), [Max Points on a Line](https://leetcode.com/problems/max-points-on-a-line/)

- Mutation drills:
  - Transform Manhattan distance by x+y and x-y.
  - Sweep one axis and maintain active intervals.
  - Coordinate compress rectangle edges.
  - Use hull/order structure for line queries.

## Advanced Techniques

### 234. [Meet in the Middle](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1628)

- Technique family: advanced bitset mitm
- Why this matters: These problems teach the bitset/mask techniques that make huge constants disappear.
- Baseline concepts: meet-in-the-middle, bitset optimization, SOS DP, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Split Array With Same Average](https://leetcode.com/problems/split-array-with-same-average/), [Partition Array Into Two Arrays to Minimize Sum Difference](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-array-into-two-arrays-to-minimize-sum-difference/), [Closest Subsequence Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/closest-subsequence-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Hamming Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2136), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Hamming Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2136), [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Corner Subgrid Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2137), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [Signal Processing](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2113)
- Mutation drills:
  - Split n into two halves.
  - Use bitset rows for fast intersections.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.
  - Transform xor/and/or subset counts.

### 240. [Cut and Paste](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2072)

- Technique family: rope treap
- Why this matters: Implicit treaps are the competitive-programming answer to mutable sequence problems.
- Baseline concepts: implicit treap, split/merge, lazy reversal, sequence data structure
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Treap (A Randomized Binary Search Tree)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/treap-a-randomized-binary-search-tree/), [Design Skiplist](https://leetcode.com/problems/design-skiplist/), [Implementation of Search, Insert and Delete in Treap](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/implementation-of-search-insert-and-delete-in-treap/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Substring Reversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2073), [Reversals and Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2074)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Substring Reversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2073), [Bit Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1188)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Reversals and Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2074), [Reversal Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2075), [Two Stacks Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2402)
- Pro solidifiers: [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428), [Reversals and Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2074)
- Mutation drills:
  - Split by position.
  - Merge two sequences.
  - Lazy reverse a range.
  - Maintain aggregate sums under sequence edits.

### 243. [Necessary Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2076)

- Technique family: advanced graph special
- Why this matters: These tasks are graph-theory depth checks beyond standard BFS/Dijkstra.
- Baseline concepts: graph theory, bridges, orientations, tree isomorphism, MST queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Critical Connections in a Network](https://leetcode.com/problems/critical-connections-in-a-network/), [Strongly Connected Components (Kosaraju's Algo)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/strongly-connected-components-kosarajus-algo/1), [Reconstruct Itinerary](https://leetcode.com/problems/reconstruct-itinerary/), [Find the Shortest Superstring](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-shortest-superstring/), [Bridge edge in a graph](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/bridge-edge-in-graph/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Acyclic Graph Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1756)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Graph Girth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1707)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Strongly Connected Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2177), [Even Outdegree Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2179), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [Tree Isomorphism II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1701), [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705)
- Mutation drills:
  - Orient edges under degree/connectivity constraints.
  - Hash trees canonically for isomorphism.
  - Answer bridge/articulation queries.
  - Classify MST edges under query sets.

### 246. [Monster Game I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2084)

- Technique family: dp optimization
- Why this matters: DP optimization is the leap from solvable but slow to accepted under hard constraints.
- Baseline concepts: convex hull trick, Li Chao tree, divide-and-conquer DP, Knuth optimization
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Burst Balloons](https://leetcode.com/problems/burst-balloons/), [Minimum Score Triangulation of Polygon](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-score-triangulation-of-polygon/), [Matrix Chain Multiplication](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-chain-multiplication0303/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Monster Game II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2085), [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Monster Game II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2085), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087), [Subarray Squares](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2086), [Apples and Bananas](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2111)
- Pro solidifiers: [Signal Processing](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2113), [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402), [Stick Difference](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3401)
- Mutation drills:
  - Derive line slope/intercept from DP.
  - Use Li Chao when queries/slopes are not monotonic.
  - Check monotone optima before D&C optimization.
  - Check Knuth conditions before using Knuth optimization.

### 247. [Monster Game II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2085)

- Technique family: dp optimization
- Why this matters: DP optimization is the leap from solvable but slow to accepted under hard constraints.
- Baseline concepts: convex hull trick, Li Chao tree, divide-and-conquer DP, Knuth optimization
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Burst Balloons](https://leetcode.com/problems/burst-balloons/), [Minimum Score Triangulation of Polygon](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-score-triangulation-of-polygon/), [Matrix Chain Multiplication](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-chain-multiplication0303/1)

- Beginner solidifiers: [Monster Game I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2084), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087), [Subarray Squares](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2086), [Apples and Bananas](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2111)
- Pro solidifiers: [Signal Processing](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2113), [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402), [Stick Difference](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3401)
- Mutation drills:
  - Derive line slope/intercept from DP.
  - Use Li Chao when queries/slopes are not monotonic.
  - Check monotone optima before D&C optimization.
  - Check Knuth conditions before using Knuth optimization.

### 252. [One Bit Positions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2112)

- Technique family: advanced bitset mitm
- Why this matters: These problems teach the bitset/mask techniques that make huge constants disappear.
- Baseline concepts: meet-in-the-middle, bitset optimization, SOS DP, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Split Array With Same Average](https://leetcode.com/problems/split-array-with-same-average/), [Partition Array Into Two Arrays to Minimize Sum Difference](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-array-into-two-arrays-to-minimize-sum-difference/), [Closest Subsequence Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/closest-subsequence-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Meet in the Middle](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1628), [Hamming Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2136), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Meet in the Middle](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1628), [Hamming Distance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2136), [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Corner Subgrid Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2137), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [Signal Processing](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2113)
- Mutation drills:
  - Split n into two halves.
  - Use bitset rows for fast intersections.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.
  - Transform xor/and/or subset counts.

### 254. [New Roads Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2101)

- Technique family: advanced graph special
- Why this matters: These tasks are graph-theory depth checks beyond standard BFS/Dijkstra.
- Baseline concepts: graph theory, bridges, orientations, tree isomorphism, MST queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Critical Connections in a Network](https://leetcode.com/problems/critical-connections-in-a-network/), [Strongly Connected Components (Kosaraju's Algo)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/strongly-connected-components-kosarajus-algo/1), [Reconstruct Itinerary](https://leetcode.com/problems/reconstruct-itinerary/), [Find the Shortest Superstring](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-shortest-superstring/), [Bridge edge in a graph](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/bridge-edge-in-graph/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Acyclic Graph Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1756)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Graph Girth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1707)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Strongly Connected Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2177), [Even Outdegree Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2179), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [Tree Isomorphism II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1701), [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705)
- Mutation drills:
  - Orient edges under degree/connectivity constraints.
  - Hash trees canonically for isomorphism.
  - Answer bridge/articulation queries.
  - Classify MST edges under query sets.

### 255. [Dynamic Connectivity](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2133)

- Technique family: mst dsu
- Why this matters: DSU starts easy and becomes a core technique for offline and graph-optimization tasks.
- Baseline concepts: DSU, Kruskal, component size, MST edge classification
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Min Cost to Connect All Points](https://leetcode.com/problems/min-cost-to-connect-all-points/), [Redundant Connection](https://leetcode.com/problems/redundant-connection/), [Minimum Spanning Tree - Kruskal's Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/minimum-spanning-tree-kruskals-algorithm/1), [Disjoint Set (Union-Find)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/disjoint-set-union-find/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676), [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666), [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407), [MST Edge Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3409)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [New Roads Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2101), [Transfer Speeds Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3111)
- Mutation drills:
  - Maintain component count and max component size.
  - Force or ban one edge in MST.
  - Process deletions offline in reverse.
  - Classify critical and optional MST edges.

### 256. [Parcel Delivery](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2121)

- Technique family: flow matching
- Why this matters: Flow is the doorway to matching, cuts, disjoint paths, and assignment-style reductions.
- Baseline concepts: max flow, min cut, bipartite matching, path decomposition
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Is Graph Bipartite?](https://leetcode.com/problems/is-graph-bipartite/), [Find the Maximum Flow](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/find-the-maximum-flow2126/1), [Maximum Bipartite Matching](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/maximum-bipartite-matching--170646/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Download Speed](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1694), [Police Chase](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1695), [School Dance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1696)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Download Speed](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1694), [School Dance](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1696), [Police Chase](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1695)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Distinct Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1711), [Grid Puzzle I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2432), [Grid Puzzle II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2131)
- Pro solidifiers: [Task Assignment](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2129), [Distinct Routes II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2130)
- Mutation drills:
  - Extract min cut after max flow.
  - Reduce matching to flow.
  - Recover actual disjoint paths.
  - Add capacities greater than one.

## Sliding Window Problems

### 259. [Sliding Window Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3220)

- Technique family: sliding window
- Why this matters: Sliding window tasks teach online maintenance of local statistics.
- Baseline concepts: fixed window, monotonic deque, ordered window, window statistics
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Longest Substring Without Repeating Characters](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-substring-without-repeating-characters/), [Minimum Window Substring](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-window-substring/), [Minimum Size Subarray Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/minimum-size-subarray-sum/), [Longest Repeating Character Replacement](https://leetcode.com/problems/longest-repeating-character-replacement/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Sliding Window Minimum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3221), [Sliding Window Distinct Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3222)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Sliding Window Minimum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3221), [Sliding Window Xor](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3426)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Sliding Window Distinct Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3222), [Sliding Window Mode](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3224), [Sliding Window Mex](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3219)
- Pro solidifiers: [Sliding Window Median](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1076), [Sliding Window Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1077), [Sliding Window Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3223)
- Mutation drills:
  - Maintain min/max with a deque.
  - Maintain median/cost with two multisets.
  - Maintain mex with frequency and missing set.
  - Support insert outgoing and incoming elements symmetrically.

  - Maintain median/cost with two multisets.
  - Maintain mex with frequency and missing set.
  - Support insert outgoing and incoming elements symmetrically.

## Interactive Problems

### 270. [Hidden Integer](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3112)

- Technique family: interactive
- Why this matters: Interactive tasks train adversarial information gathering, not just offline computation.
- Baseline concepts: interactive protocol, query strategy, binary search, information theory
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Guess Number Higher or Lower](https://leetcode.com/problems/guess-number-higher-or-lower/), [Guess the Word](https://leetcode.com/problems/guess-the-word/), [Find the Celebrity](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-celebrity/)

- Beginner solidifiers: [Hidden Permutation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3139), [Permuted Binary Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3228)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [K-th Highest Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3305), [Colored Chairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3273), [Inversion Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3140)
- Pro solidifiers: [Inversion Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3140), [Permuted Binary Strings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3228), [Colored Chairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3273)
- Mutation drills:
  - Minimize number of queries.
  - Flush output after every query.
  - Treat judge answers as constraints.
  - Design strategy before coding protocol details.

## Bitwise Operations

### 276. [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146)

- Technique family: bitwise operations
- Why this matters: Bitwise problems often require algebraic structure, not brute force over bits.
- Baseline concepts: xor basis, bit DP, prefix xor, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Xor Pyramid Peak](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2419)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

### 278. [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191)

- Technique family: bitwise operations
- Why this matters: Bitwise problems often require algebraic structure, not brute force over bits.
- Baseline concepts: xor basis, bit DP, prefix xor, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)

- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Xor Pyramid Peak](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2419)

- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

## Construction Problems

### 287. [Inverse Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2214)

- Technique family: construction
- Why this matters: Construction problems train proof-first thinking and are common in contests.
- Baseline concepts: constructive proof, permutations, invariants, existence conditions
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [DI String Match](https://leetcode.com/problems/di-string-match/), [Reveal Cards In Increasing Order](https://leetcode.com/problems/reveal-cards-in-increasing-order/), [Beautiful Arrangement](https://leetcode.com/problems/beautiful-arrangement/), [Construct the Rectangle](https://leetcode.com/problems/construct-the-rectangle/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Monotone Subsequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2215), [Beautiful Permutation II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3175)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Monotone Subsequences](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2215), [Chess Tournament](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1697)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Third Permutation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3422), [Permutation Prime Sums](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3423), [Filling Trominos](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2423)
- Pro solidifiers: [Grid Path Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2418), [Distinct Sums Grid](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3424), [Two Stacks Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2402)
- Mutation drills:
  - Prove impossible cases.
  - Preserve invariant while constructing.
  - Build greedily and verify constraints.
  - Construct lexicographically smallest/largest version.

- Mutation drills:
  - Prove impossible cases.
  - Preserve invariant while constructing.
  - Build greedily and verify constraints.
  - Construct lexicographically smallest/largest version.

### 294. [Grid Path Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2418)

- Technique family: construction
- Why this matters: Construction problems train proof-first thinking and are common in contests.
- Baseline concepts: constructive proof, permutations, invariants, existence conditions
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [DI String Match](https://leetcode.com/problems/di-string-match/), [Reveal Cards In Increasing Order](https://leetcode.com/problems/reveal-cards-in-increasing-order/), [Beautiful Arrangement](https://leetcode.com/problems/beautiful-arrangement/), [Construct the Rectangle](https://leetcode.com/problems/construct-the-rectangle/)

- Pro solidifiers: [Distinct Sums Grid](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3424), [Two Stacks Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2402)
- Mutation drills:
  - Prove impossible cases.
  - Preserve invariant while constructing.
  - Build greedily and verify constraints.
  - Construct lexicographically smallest/largest version.

## Advanced Graph Problems

### 295. [Nearest Shops](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3303)

- Technique family: advanced graph special
- Why this matters: These tasks are graph-theory depth checks beyond standard BFS/Dijkstra.
- Baseline concepts: graph theory, bridges, orientations, tree isomorphism, MST queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Critical Connections in a Network](https://leetcode.com/problems/critical-connections-in-a-network/), [Strongly Connected Components (Kosaraju's Algo)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/strongly-connected-components-kosarajus-algo/1), [Reconstruct Itinerary](https://leetcode.com/problems/reconstruct-itinerary/), [Find the Shortest Superstring](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-shortest-superstring/), [Bridge edge in a graph](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/bridge-edge-in-graph/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Acyclic Graph Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1756)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Graph Girth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1707)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Strongly Connected Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2177), [Even Outdegree Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2179), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [Tree Isomorphism II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1701), [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705)
- Mutation drills:
  - Orient edges under degree/connectivity constraints.
  - Hash trees canonically for isomorphism.
  - Answer bridge/articulation queries.
  - Classify MST edges under query sets.

### 298. [Course Schedule II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1757)

- Technique family: graph dag toposort
- Why this matters: DAG DP is the bridge between graph traversal and dynamic programming.
- Baseline concepts: topological sort, DAG DP, cycle detection, path counting
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Course Schedule](https://leetcode.com/problems/course-schedule/), [Course Schedule II](https://leetcode.com/problems/course-schedule-ii/), [Find Eventual Safe States](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-eventual-safe-states/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Course Schedule](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1679), [Longest Flight Route](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1680), [Game Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1681)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Course Schedule](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1679), [Round Trip II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1678), [Longest Flight Route](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1680)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Game Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1681), [Acyclic Graph Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1756)
- Pro solidifiers: [Coin Collector](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1686), [Fixed Length Walk Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3357), [Visiting Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1203)
- Mutation drills:
  - Return order, longest path, or path count.
  - Detect cycles before DP.
  - Condense SCCs to create a DAG.
  - Use topo order from indegrees or DFS finish time.

### 303. [Fixed Length Walk Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3357)

- Technique family: matrix probability games
- Why this matters: This section ties math, DP, and game theory into compact but deep tasks.
- Baseline concepts: matrix exponentiation, linear recurrences, probability DP, Grundy/nim
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Nim Game](https://leetcode.com/problems/nim-game/), [Stone Game](https://leetcode.com/problems/stone-game/), [New 21 Game](https://leetcode.com/problems/new-21-game/), [Matrix Exponentiation](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/matrix-exponentiation2711/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Fibonacci Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1722), [Throwing Dice](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1096), [Dice Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1725)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Fibonacci Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1722), [Throwing Dice](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1096), [Dice Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1725)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Graph Paths I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1723), [Graph Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1724), [Moving Robots](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1726)
- Pro solidifiers: [System of Linear Equations](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3154), [Inversion Probability](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1728), [Grundy's Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2207)
- Mutation drills:
  - Turn recurrence into matrix transitions.
  - Use min-plus multiplication for shortest path counts/costs.
  - Compute expectation/probability by state DP.
  - Use xor of Grundy numbers for impartial games.

### 304. [Transfer Speeds Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3111)

- Technique family: matrix probability games
- Why this matters: This section ties math, DP, and game theory into compact but deep tasks.

### 305. [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407)

- Technique family: mst dsu
- Why this matters: DSU starts easy and becomes a core technique for offline and graph-optimization tasks.
- Baseline concepts: DSU, Kruskal, component size, MST edge classification
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Min Cost to Connect All Points](https://leetcode.com/problems/min-cost-to-connect-all-points/), [Redundant Connection](https://leetcode.com/problems/redundant-connection/), [Minimum Spanning Tree - Kruskal's Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/minimum-spanning-tree-kruskals-algorithm/1), [Disjoint Set (Union-Find)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/disjoint-set-union-find/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676), [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666), [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Network Breakdown](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1677), [MST Edge Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3409)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [New Roads Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2101), [Transfer Speeds Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3111)
- Mutation drills:
  - Maintain component count and max component size.
  - Force or ban one edge in MST.
  - Process deletions offline in reverse.
  - Classify critical and optional MST edges.

- Technique family: mst dsu
- Why this matters: DSU starts easy and becomes a core technique for offline and graph-optimization tasks.
- Baseline concepts: DSU, Kruskal, component size, MST edge classification
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Min Cost to Connect All Points](https://leetcode.com/problems/min-cost-to-connect-all-points/), [Redundant Connection](https://leetcode.com/problems/redundant-connection/), [Minimum Spanning Tree - Kruskal's Algorithm](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/minimum-spanning-tree-kruskals-algorithm/1), [Disjoint Set (Union-Find)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/disjoint-set-union-find/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Building Roads](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1666), [Road Reparation](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1675), [Road Construction](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1676)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407), [MST Edge Cost](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3409)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [New Roads Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2101), [Transfer Speeds Sum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3111)
- Mutation drills:
  - Maintain component count and max component size.
  - Force or ban one edge in MST.
  - Process deletions offline in reverse.
  - Classify critical and optional MST edges.

- Beginner solidifiers: [Prüfer Code](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1134), [Tree Traversals](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1702), [Graph Girth](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1707)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Strongly Connected Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2177), [Even Outdegree Edges](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2179), [MST Edge Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3407)
- Pro solidifiers: [MST Edge Set Check](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3408), [Tree Isomorphism II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1701), [Forbidden Cities](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1705)
- Mutation drills:
  - Orient edges under degree/connectivity constraints.
  - Hash trees canonically for isomorphism.
  - Answer bridge/articulation queries.
  - Classify MST edges under query sets.

### 322. [New Flight Routes](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1685)

- Technique family: advanced graph special
- Why this matters: These tasks are graph-theory depth checks beyond standard BFS/Dijkstra.
- Baseline concepts: graph theory, bridges, orientations, tree isomorphism, MST queries
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Critical Connections in a Network](https://leetcode.com/problems/critical-connections-in-a-network/), [Strongly Connected Components (Kosaraju's Algo)](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/strongly-connected-components-kosarajus-algo/1), [Reconstruct Itinerary](https://leetcode.com/problems/reconstruct-itinerary/), [Find the Shortest Superstring](https://leetcode.com/problems/find-the-shortest-superstring/), [Bridge edge in a graph](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/bridge-edge-in-graph/1)

## Counting Problems

### 323. [Filled Subgrid Count I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3413)

- Technique family: counting advanced
- Why this matters: Advanced counting is where formulas, DP, and combinatorics start to merge.
- Baseline concepts: combinatorics, DP counting, grid/subgrid counting, distributions
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Unique Paths](https://leetcode.com/problems/unique-paths/), [Unique Binary Search Trees](https://leetcode.com/problems/unique-binary-search-trees/), [Count All Valid Pickup and Delivery Options](https://leetcode.com/problems/count-all-valid-pickup-and-delivery-options/), [nCr mod M | Part 1](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/ncr-mod-m-part-10038/1), [Queries of nCr%p in O(1) time complexity](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/dsa/queries-of-ncrp-in-o1-time-complexity/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080), [Permutation Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2229)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Filled Subgrid Count II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3414), [Empty String](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1080)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Permutation Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2229), [Counting Bishops](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2176), [Grid Paths II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1078)
- Pro solidifiers: [Grid Completion](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2429), [Tournament Graph Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3232), [Functional Graph Distribution](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2415)
- Mutation drills:
  - Count objects by contribution instead of enumeration.
  - Use DP over positions and counts.
  - Exploit symmetry/distribution.
  - Apply inclusion-exclusion when constraints overlap.

- Mutation drills:
  - Count objects by contribution instead of enumeration.
  - Use DP over positions and counts.
  - Exploit symmetry/distribution.
  - Apply inclusion-exclusion when constraints overlap.

## Additional Problems I

### 341. [Shortest Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1087)

- Technique family: additional mixed
- Why this matters: The additional sections are deliberately mixed; recognition is the skill being trained.
- Baseline concepts: mixed technique recognition, reduction, binary search, data structures, DP
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Two Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/two-sum/), [Best Time to Buy and Sell Stock](https://leetcode.com/problems/best-time-to-buy-and-sell-stock/), [Maximum Subarray](https://leetcode.com/problems/maximum-subarray/), [Number of Islands](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-islands/), [Climbing Stairs](https://leetcode.com/problems/climbing-stairs/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Swap Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1670), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Swap Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1670), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Bubble Sort Rounds II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3152), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Bit Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1188)
- Pro solidifiers: [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301), [K Subset Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3109), [Coding Company](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1665)
- Mutation drills:
  - Identify the hidden primary technique.
  - Try both direct and transformed state.
  - Look for monotonicity, order, or contribution.
  - After solving, classify the task into a reusable pattern.

### 346. [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)

- Technique family: binary search answer
- Why this matters: Parametric search turns many impossible-looking optimization tasks into clean decision problems.
- Baseline concepts: binary search on answer, monotonic feasibility, count <= x
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Binary Search](https://leetcode.com/problems/binary-search/), [Koko Eating Bananas](https://leetcode.com/problems/koko-eating-bananas/), [Capacity To Ship Packages Within D Days](https://leetcode.com/problems/capacity-to-ship-packages-within-d-days/), [Split Array Largest Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/split-array-largest-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620), [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620), [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301), [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [K-th Highest Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3305)
- Pro solidifiers: [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088), [Lines and Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3430)
- Mutation drills:
  - Minimize maximum vs maximize minimum.
  - Prove the feasibility predicate is monotonic.
  - Use counting <= mid instead of direct index search.
  - Binary search real values and control precision.

### 354. [Square Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3193)

- Technique family: bitwise operations
- Why this matters: Bitwise problems often require algebraic structure, not brute force over bits.
- Baseline concepts: xor basis, bit DP, prefix xor, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)

- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

### 359. [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301)

- Technique family: binary search answer
- Why this matters: Parametric search turns many impossible-looking optimization tasks into clean decision problems.
- Baseline concepts: binary search on answer, monotonic feasibility, count <= x
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Binary Search](https://leetcode.com/problems/binary-search/), [Koko Eating Bananas](https://leetcode.com/problems/koko-eating-bananas/), [Capacity To Ship Packages Within D Days](https://leetcode.com/problems/capacity-to-ship-packages-within-d-days/), [Split Array Largest Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/split-array-largest-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620), [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620), [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086), [K-th Highest Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3305)
- Pro solidifiers: [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088), [Lines and Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3430)
- Mutation drills:
  - Minimize maximum vs maximize minimum.
  - Prove the feasibility predicate is monotonic.
  - Use counting <= mid instead of direct index search.
  - Binary search real values and control precision.

- Pro solidifiers: [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301), [K Subset Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3109), [Coding Company](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1665)
- Mutation drills:
  - Identify the hidden primary technique.
  - Try both direct and transformed state.
  - Look for monotonicity, order, or contribution.
  - After solving, classify the task into a reusable pattern.

### 364. [Bit Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1188)

- Technique family: bitwise operations
- Why this matters: Bitwise problems often require algebraic structure, not brute force over bits.
- Baseline concepts: xor basis, bit DP, prefix xor, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Xor Pyramid Peak](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2419)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

### 365. [Writing Numbers](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1086)

- Technique family: binary search answer
- Why this matters: Parametric search turns many impossible-looking optimization tasks into clean decision problems.
- Baseline concepts: binary search on answer, monotonic feasibility, count <= x
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Binary Search](https://leetcode.com/problems/binary-search/), [Koko Eating Bananas](https://leetcode.com/problems/koko-eating-bananas/), [Capacity To Ship Packages Within D Days](https://leetcode.com/problems/capacity-to-ship-packages-within-d-days/), [Split Array Largest Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/split-array-largest-sum/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620), [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Factory Machines](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1620), [Array Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1085), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301), [K-th Highest Score](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3305)
- Pro solidifiers: [Houses and Schools](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2087), [Knuth Division](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2088), [Lines and Queries II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3430)
- Mutation drills:
  - Minimize maximum vs maximize minimum.
  - Prove the feasibility predicate is monotonic.
  - Use counting <= mid instead of direct index search.
  - Binary search real values and control precision.

### 367. [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147)

- Technique family: monotonic stack
- Why this matters: Monotonic structures are the hidden engine behind many hard linear-time solutions.
- Baseline concepts: monotonic stack, nearest smaller/greater, histogram rectangles, contribution counting
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Next Greater Element I](https://leetcode.com/problems/next-greater-element-i/), [Daily Temperatures](https://leetcode.com/problems/daily-temperatures/), [Largest Rectangle in Histogram](https://leetcode.com/problems/largest-rectangle-in-histogram/), [Trapping Rain Water](https://leetcode.com/problems/trapping-rain-water/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Sliding Window Minimum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3221)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Building II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1148), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425)
- Pro solidifiers: [Subarray Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1190), [Visible Buildings Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3304), [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch nearest smaller to nearest greater.
  - Handle equal values with strict vs non-strict comparisons.
  - Return boundaries for each index.
  - Convert a grid/sequence into repeated histogram states.

### 389. [Bit Substrings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2115)

- Technique family: bitwise operations
- Why this matters: Bitwise problems often require algebraic structure, not brute force over bits.
- Baseline concepts: xor basis, bit DP, prefix xor, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Xor Pyramid Peak](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2419)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Xor Pyramid Peak](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2419)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

### 393. [Minimum Cost Pairs](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3402)

- Technique family: additional mixed
- Why this matters: The additional sections are deliberately mixed; recognition is the skill being trained.
- Baseline concepts: mixed technique recognition, reduction, binary search, data structures, DP
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Two Sum](https://leetcode.com/problems/two-sum/), [Best Time to Buy and Sell Stock](https://leetcode.com/problems/best-time-to-buy-and-sell-stock/), [Maximum Subarray](https://leetcode.com/problems/maximum-subarray/), [Number of Islands](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-islands/), [Climbing Stairs](https://leetcode.com/problems/climbing-stairs/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Shortest Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1087), [Swap Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1670), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Shortest Subsequence](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1087), [Swap Game](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1670), [Multiplication Table](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2422)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Bubble Sort Rounds II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3152), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Bit Inversions](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1188)
- Pro solidifiers: [Maximum Average Subarrays](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3301), [K Subset Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3109), [Coding Company](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1665)
- Mutation drills:
  - Identify the hidden primary technique.
  - Try both direct and transformed state.
  - Look for monotonicity, order, or contribution.
  - After solving, classify the task into a reusable pattern.

### 394. [Same Sum Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3425)

- Technique family: bitwise operations
- Why this matters: Bitwise problems often require algebraic structure, not brute force over bits.
- Baseline concepts: xor basis, bit DP, prefix xor, subset transforms
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Single Number](https://leetcode.com/problems/single-number/), [Number of 1 Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/number-of-1-bits/), [Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/subsets/), [Sum of Two Integers](https://leetcode.com/problems/sum-of-two-integers/), [Counting Bits](https://leetcode.com/problems/counting-bits/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Counting Bits](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1146), [Maximum Xor Subarray](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1655), [Xor Pyramid Peak](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2419)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Xor Subset](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3191), [Number of Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3211), [SOS Bit Problem](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1654)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3192), [All Subarray Xors](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3233), [And Subset Count](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3141)
- Mutation drills:
  - Use prefix xor for subarray xor.
  - Build linear basis for maximum xor subset.
  - Count subset xors with rank.
  - Run SOS DP over masks.

### 395. [Mex Grid Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1157)

- Technique family: dp bitmask profile
- Why this matters: Bitmask and profile DP are the bridge into serious competitive-programming DP.
- Baseline concepts: bitmask DP, subset DP, profile DP, state compression
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Beautiful Arrangement](https://leetcode.com/problems/beautiful-arrangement/), [Partition to K Equal Sum Subsets](https://leetcode.com/problems/partition-to-k-equal-sum-subsets/), [Parallel Courses II](https://leetcode.com/problems/parallel-courses-ii/), [Travelling Salesman Problem](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/problems/travelling-salesman-problem2732/1)
- Prerequisite runway: [Elevator Rides](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1653), [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [Hamiltonian Flights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1690)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Elevator Rides](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1653), [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [School Excursion](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1706)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Hamiltonian Flights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1690), [Counting Tilings](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2181), [K Subset Sums I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3108)
- Pro solidifiers: [K Subset Sums II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3109), [Grid Puzzle II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2131), [Same Sum Subsets](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3425)
- Mutation drills:
  - Mask represents used items, skills, or frontier cells.
  - Iterate submasks efficiently.
  - Precompute transitions or subset scores.
  - Reconstruct the chosen subset/path.

### 396. [Maximum Building II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1148)

- Technique family: monotonic stack
- Why this matters: Monotonic structures are the hidden engine behind many hard linear-time solutions.
- Baseline concepts: monotonic stack, nearest smaller/greater, histogram rectangles, contribution counting
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Next Greater Element I](https://leetcode.com/problems/next-greater-element-i/), [Daily Temperatures](https://leetcode.com/problems/daily-temperatures/), [Largest Rectangle in Histogram](https://leetcode.com/problems/largest-rectangle-in-histogram/), [Trapping Rain Water](https://leetcode.com/problems/trapping-rain-water/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Sliding Window Minimum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3221)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425)
- Pro solidifiers: [Subarray Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1190), [Visible Buildings Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3304), [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch nearest smaller to nearest greater.
  - Handle equal values with strict vs non-strict comparisons.
  - Return boundaries for each index.
  - Convert a grid/sequence into repeated histogram states.

### 400. [Two Stacks Sorting](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2402)

- Technique family: monotonic stack
- Why this matters: Monotonic structures are the hidden engine behind many hard linear-time solutions.
- Baseline concepts: monotonic stack, nearest smaller/greater, histogram rectangles, contribution counting
- External prereqs (LC/GFG): [Next Greater Element I](https://leetcode.com/problems/next-greater-element-i/), [Daily Temperatures](https://leetcode.com/problems/daily-temperatures/), [Largest Rectangle in Histogram](https://leetcode.com/problems/largest-rectangle-in-histogram/), [Trapping Rain Water](https://leetcode.com/problems/trapping-rain-water/)
- Prerequisite runway: [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147)
- Beginner solidifiers: [Nearest Smaller Values](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1645), [Advertisement](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1142), [Sliding Window Minimum](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3221)
- Intermediate solidifiers: [Maximum Building I](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1147), [Maximum Building II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1148), [Stack Weights](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/2425)
- Pro solidifiers: [Subarray Sum Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/1190), [Visible Buildings Queries](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3304), [Line Segments Trace II](https://cses.fi/problemset/task/3428)
- Mutation drills:
  - Switch nearest smaller to nearest greater.
  - Handle equal values with strict vs non-strict comparisons.
  - Return boundaries for each index.
  - Convert a grid/sequence into repeated histogram states.

## Progression After Finishing CSES

1. Redo the problems you failed using the 1/3/7/14/30/60 day schedule.
2. Move from CSES Graph Algorithms to CSES Advanced Graph Problems again; this is where a lot of hidden growth lives.
3. Do AtCoder Educational DP Contest for DP fluency.
4. Use USACO Guide Gold/Platinum for topic-deepening.
5. Start Codeforces 1600-1900 for pattern recognition, then 2000-2400 for synthesis.
6. Revisit cp-algorithms for any topic where you can solve but cannot prove correctness.

## External Reference Trail

- [CSES Problem Set](https://cses.fi/problemset/)
- [cp-algorithms](https://cp-algorithms.com/)
- [USACO Guide](https://usaco.guide/)
- [AtCoder Educational DP Contest](https://atcoder.jp/contests/dp/tasks)
- [Codeforces](https://codeforces.com/)
